  • ion/Class.ts
    "
    export type Class = any & {
        id: string
        implements: string[]
    }

    export function isInstance(_class: Class, instance) {
        if (instance != null) {
            let _implements = instance.constructor as Set<string> | undefined
            if (_implements) {
                return _implements.has(_class.id)
            }
        }
        return false
    }

    import * as Number from './Number';
    export type Integer = Number.Number;
    export function isInteger(value): value is Integer {
        return Number.isNumber(value) && value % 1 === 0;

  • ion/Type.ts
    "/*
    This file was generated from ion source. Do not edit.
    */
    import * as String from './String';
    import * as Class from './Class';
    export class Type {
        readonly id: String.String;
        constructor({id}: { id: String.String }) {
            if (!String.isString(id))
                throw new Error('id is not a String: ' + id);
            this.id = id;
        }
        static is(value): value is Type {
            return isType(value);
        }
    }
    Type['id'] = 'ion_Type';
    Type['implements'] = new Set(['ion_Type']);
    export const isType = function (value): value is Type {
        return Class.isInstance(Type, value);
    };"

  • sample/Point2.ts
    "/*
    This file was generated from ion source. Do not edit.
    */
    import * as Integer from '../ion/Integer';
    import * as Class from '../ion/Class';
    export type Whole = Integer.Integer;
    export function isWhole(value): value is Whole {
        return Integer.isInteger(value) && value >= 0;
    }
    export class Point2 {
        readonly x: Whole;
        readonly y: Whole;
        constructor(x: Whole = 0, y: Whole = 0) {
            if (!isWhole(x))
                throw new Error('x is not a Whole: ' + x);
            if (!isWhole(y))
                throw new Error('y is not a Whole: ' + y);
            this.x = x;
            this.y = y;
        }
        static is(value): value is Point2 {
            return isPoint2(value);
        }
    }
    Point2['id'] = 'sample_Point2';
    Point2['implements'] = new Set(['sample_Point2']);
    export const isPoint2 = function (value): value is Point2 {
        return Class.isInstance(Point2, value);
    };"

        readonly z: Point2.Whole;

            if (!Point2.isWhole(x))
                throw new Error('x is not a Whole: ' + x);
            if (!Point2.isWhole(y))
                throw new Error('y is not a Whole: ' + y);
            if (!Point2.isWhole(z))
                throw new Error('z is not a Whole: ' + z);
            this.x = x;
            this.y = y;
            this.z = z;

        static is(value): value is Point3 {

    import * as Point3 from './Point3';
    import * as Point2 from './Point2';
    import * as String from '../ion/String';
    import * as Class from '../ion/Class';
    export class PointClass {
        readonly x: Point2.Whole;
        readonly y: Point2.Whole;
        readonly z: Point2.Whole;
        readonly name: String.String;
        constructor({x = 0, y = 0, z, name}: {
            x?: Point2.Whole,
            y?: Point2.Whole,
            z: Point2.Whole,
            name: String.String
        }) {
            if (!Point2.isWhole(x))
                throw new Error('x is not a Whole: ' + x);
            if (!Point2.isWhole(y))
                throw new Error('y is not a Whole: ' + y);
            if (!Point2.isWhole(z))
                throw new Error('z is not a Whole: ' + z);
            if (!String.isString(name))
                throw new Error('name is not a String: ' + name);
            this.x = x;
            this.y = y;
            this.z = z;
            this.name = name;
        }
        static is(value): value is PointClass {
            return isPointClass(value);
        }
    }
    PointClass['id'] = 'sample_PointClass';
    PointClass['implements'] = new Set([
        'sample_PointClass',
        'sample_Point3',
        'sample_Point2'
    ]);
    export const isPointClass = function (value): value is PointClass {
        return Class.isInstance(PointClass, value);

  • ion/Class.ts
    "
    export type Class = any & {
        id: string
        implements: string[]
    }

    export function isInstance(_class: Class, instance) {
        if (instance != null) {
            let _implements = instance.constructor as Set<string> | undefined
            if (_implements) {
                return _implements.has(_class.id)
            }
        }
        return false
    }
    "

    "/*
    This file was generated from ion source. Do not edit.

    import * as String from './String';
    import * as Class from './Class';
    export class Type {
        readonly id: String.String;
        constructor({id}: { id: String.String }) {
            if (!String.isString(id))
                throw new Error('id is not a String: ' + id);
            this.id = id;
        }
        static is(value): value is Type {
            return isType(value);
        }
    }
    Type['id'] = 'ion_Type';
    Type['implements'] = new Set(['ion_Type']);
    export const isType = function (value): value is Type {
        return Class.isInstance(Type, value);
    };"

    import * as Point2 from './Point2';
    import * as String from '../ion/String';
    import * as Class from '../ion/Class';
    export class PointClass {
        readonly x: Point2.Whole;
        readonly y: Point2.Whole;
        readonly z: Point2.Whole;
        readonly name: String.String;
        constructor({x = 0, y = 0, z, name}: {
            x?: Point2.Whole,
            y?: Point2.Whole,
            z: Point2.Whole,
            name: String.String
        }) {
            if (!Point2.isWhole(x))
                throw new Error('x is not a Whole: ' + x);
            if (!Point2.isWhole(y))
                throw new Error('y is not a Whole: ' + y);
            if (!Point2.isWhole(z))
                throw new Error('z is not a Whole: ' + z);
            if (!String.isString(name))
                throw new Error('name is not a String: ' + name);
            this.x = x;
            this.y = y;
            this.z = z;
            this.name = name;
        }
        static is(value): value is PointClass {
            return isPointClass(value);
        }
    }
